<pr_description>
v2.17.0 breaks custom_resource_config_file config option
**What happened**:

Updating to kube-state-metrics version 2.17.0 broke the `custom_resource_config_file` configuration option in `config.yaml`

**What you expected to happen**:

```
    custom_resource_config_file: "/etc/kube-state-metrics/custom-resource-config.yaml"
```

to be equivalent to 

```
--custom-resource-state-config-file=/etc/kube-state-metrics/custom-resource-config.yaml
```

like in prior versions.

**How to reproduce it (as minimally and precisely as possible)**:

```bash
minikube start
...

helm install \
  cert-manager oci://quay.io/jetstack/charts/cert-manager \
  --version v1.19.1 \
  --namespace cert-manager \
  --create-namespace \
  --set crds.enabled=true
```

If you `git checkout v2.16.0` and follow these steps you will see a log line like:

```
I1029 16:54:39.268274  516434 config.go:85] "Using custom resource plural" resource="cert-manager.io_v1_CertificateRequest" plural="certificaterequests"
I1029 16:54:39.268824  516434 custom_resource_metrics.go:79] "Custom resource state added metrics" familyNames=["certmanager_certificaterequest_creation_time"]
I1029 16:54:39.269603  516434 builder.go:294] "Active resources" activeStoreNames="cert-manager.io/v1, Resource=certificaterequests,[...]"
```

and will see metrics like

```
$ curl -sSLf1 http://localhost:8080/metrics | grep '^certmanager_certificaterequest_creation_time'
...
certmanager_certificaterequest_creation_time{certificaterequest="my-ca-cr",customresource_group="cert-manager.io",customresource_kind="CertificateRequest",customresource_version="v1",namespace="default"} 1.76170942e+09
...
```

If you check out `main` or `v2.17.0` you will not see such output.

```
$ curl -sSLf1 http://localhost:8080/metrics | grep 'my-ca-cr'
$
```

If you append `--custom-resource-state-config-file=./custom-resource-config.yaml` to the CLI in v2.17.0, the CRs will be detected again.


**Anything else we need to know?**:

Works on v2.16.0 breaks on v2.17.0

Strongly suspect regression in one of

*  https://github.com/kubernetes/kube-state-metrics/pull/2705
* https://github.com/kubernetes/kube-state-metrics/pull/2703

    33	// MetricSet represents a collection which has a unique set of metrics.
    34	type MetricSet map[string]struct{}
    35	
    36	func (ms *MetricSet) String() string {
    37	        s := *ms
    38	        ss := s.asSlice()
    39	        sort.Strings(ss)
    40	        return strings.Join(ss, ",")
    41	}
    42	
    43	// Set converts a comma-separated string of metrics into a slice and appends it to the MetricSet.
    44	func (ms *MetricSet) Set(value string) error {
    45	        s := *ms
    46	        metrics := strings.Split(value, ",")
    47	        for _, metric := range metrics {
    48	                metric = strings.TrimSpace(metric)
    49	                if len(metric) != 0 {
    50	                        s[metric] = struct{}{}
    51	                }
    52	        }
    53	        return nil
    54	}
    55	
    56	// asSlice returns the MetricSet in the form of plain string slice.
    57	func (ms MetricSet) asSlice() []string {
    58	        metrics := make([]string, 0, len(ms))
    59	        for metric := range ms {
    60	                metrics = append(metrics, metric)
    61	        }
    62	        return metrics
    63	}

    66	func (ms *MetricSet) Type() string {
    67	        return "string"

   121	// GetNodeFieldSelector returns a nodename field selector.
   122	func (n *NodeType) GetNodeFieldSelector() string {
   123	        if string(*n) != "" {
   124	                return fields.OneTermEqualSelector("spec.nodeName", string(*n)).String()
   125	        }
   126	        return EmptyFieldSelector()
   127	}
   128	
   129	// EmptyFieldSelector returns an empty field selector.
   130	func EmptyFieldSelector() string {
   131	        return fields.Nothing().String()
   132	}
   133	
   134	// MergeFieldSelectors returns AND of a list of field selectors.
   135	func MergeFieldSelectors(selectors []string) (string, error) {
   136	        var err error
   137	        merged := EmptyFieldSelector()
   138	        for _, s := range selectors {
   139	                merged, err = MergeTwoFieldSelectors(merged, s)
   140	                if err != nil {
   141	                        return "", err
   142	                }
   143	        }
   144	        return merged, nil
   145	}
   146	
   147	// MergeTwoFieldSelectors returns AND of two field selectors.
   148	func MergeTwoFieldSelectors(s1 string, s2 string) (string, error) {
   149	        selector1, err := fields.ParseSelector(s1)
   150	        if err != nil {
   151	                return EmptyFieldSelector(), err
   152	        }
   153	        selector2, err := fields.ParseSelector(s2)
   154	        if err != nil {
   155	                return EmptyFieldSelector(), err
   156	        }
   157	        if selector1.Empty() {
   158	                return selector2.String(), nil
   159	        }
   160	        if selector2.Empty() {
   161	                return selector1.String(), nil
   162	        }
   163	        return fields.AndSelectors(selector1, selector2).String(), nil
   164	}

   167	type NamespaceList []string
   168	
   169	func (n *NamespaceList) String() string {
   170	        return strings.Join(*n, ",")
   171	}
   172	
   173	// IsAllNamespaces checks if the Namespace selector is that of `NamespaceAll` which is used for
   174	// selecting or filtering across all namespaces.
   175	func (n *NamespaceList) IsAllNamespaces() bool {
   176	        return len(*n) == 1 && (*n)[0] == metav1.NamespaceAll
   177	}
   178	
   179	// Set converts a comma-separated string of namespaces into a slice and appends it to the NamespaceList
   180	func (n *NamespaceList) Set(value string) error {
   181	        splitNamespaces := strings.Split(value, ",")
   182	        for _, ns := range splitNamespaces {
   183	                ns = strings.TrimSpace(ns)
   184	                if len(ns) != 0 {
   185	                        *n = append(*n, ns)
   186	                }
   187	        }
   188	        return nil
   189	}
   190	
   191	// GetNamespaces is a helper function to get namespaces from opts.Namespaces
   192	func (n *NamespaceList) GetNamespaces() NamespaceList {
   193	        ns := *n
   194	        if len(*n) == 0 {
   195	                klog.InfoS("Using all namespaces")
   196	                ns = DefaultNamespaces
   197	        } else {
   198	                if n.IsAllNamespaces() {
   199	                        klog.InfoS("Using all namespaces")
   200	                } else {
   201	                        klog.InfoS("Using namespaces", "nameSpaces", ns)
   202	                }
   203	        }
   204	        return ns
   205	}
   206	
   207	// GetExcludeNSFieldSelector will return excluded namespace field selector
   208	// if nsDenylist = {case1,case2}, the result will be "metadata.namespace!=case1,metadata.namespace!=case2".
   209	func (n *NamespaceList) GetExcludeNSFieldSelector(nsDenylist []string) string {
   210	        if len(nsDenylist) == 0 {
   211	                return ""
   212	        }
   213	
   214	        namespaceExcludeSelectors := make([]fields.Selector, len(nsDenylist))
   215	        for i, ns := range nsDenylist {
   216	                selector := fields.OneTermNotEqualSelector("metadata.namespace", ns)
   217	                namespaceExcludeSelectors[i] = selector
   218	        }
   219	        return fields.AndSelectors(namespaceExcludeSelectors...).String()
   220	}
   221

   223	func (n *NamespaceList) Type() string {
   224	        return "string"
   225	}

   227	// LabelWildcard allowlists any label
   228	const LabelWildcard = "*"
   229	
   230	// LabelsAllowList represents a list of allowed labels for metrics.
   231	type LabelsAllowList map[string][]string
   232	
   233	// Set converts a comma-separated string of resources and their allowed Kubernetes labels and appends to the LabelsAllowList.
   234	// Value is in the following format:
   235	// resource=[k8s-label-name,another-k8s-label],another-resource[k8s-label]
   236	// Example: pods=[app.kubernetes.io/component,app],resource=[blah]
   237	func (l *LabelsAllowList) Set(value string) error {
   238	        // Taken from text/scanner EOF constant.
   239	        const EOF = -1
   240	        var (
   241	                m            = make(map[string][]string, len(*l))
   242	                previous     rune
   243	                next         rune
   244	                firstWordPos int
   245	                name         string
   246	        )
   247	        firstWordPos = 0
   248	
   249	        for i, v := range value {
   250	                if i+1 == len(value) {
   251	                        next = EOF
   252	                } else {
   253	                        next = []rune(value)[i+1]
   254	                }
   255	                if i-1 >= 0 {
   256	                        previous = []rune(value)[i-1]
   257	                } else {
   258	                        previous = v
   259	                }
   260	
   261	                switch v {
   262	                case '=':
   263	                        if previous == ',' || next != '[' {
   264	                                return errLabelsAllowListFormat
   265	                        }
   266	                        name = strings.TrimSpace(string(([]rune(value)[firstWordPos:i])))
   267	                        m[name] = []string{}
   268	                        firstWordPos = i + 1
   269	                case '[':
   270	                        if previous != '=' {
   271	                                return errLabelsAllowListFormat
   272	                        }
   273	                        firstWordPos = i + 1
   274	                case ']':
   275	                        // if after metric group, has char not comma or end.
   276	                        if next != EOF && next != ',' {
   277	                                return errLabelsAllowListFormat
   278	                        }
   279	                        if previous != '[' {
   280	                                m[name] = append(m[name], strings.TrimSpace(string(([]rune(value)[firstWordPos:i]))))
   281	                        }
   282	                        firstWordPos = i + 1
   283	                case ',':
   284	                        // if starts or ends with comma
   285	                        if previous == v || next == EOF || next == ']' {
   286	                                return errLabelsAllowListFormat
   287	                        }
   288	                        if previous != ']' {
   289	                                m[name] = append(m[name], strings.TrimSpace(string(([]rune(value)[firstWordPos:i]))))
   290	                        }
   291	                        firstWordPos = i + 1
   292	                }
   293	        }
   294	        *l = m
   295	        return nil
   296	}
   297	
   298	// asSlice returns the LabelsAllowList in the form of plain string slice.
   299	func (l LabelsAllowList) asSlice() []string {
   300	        metrics := make([]string, 0, len(l))
   301	        for metric := range l {
   302	                metrics = append(metrics, metric)
   303	        }
   304	        return metrics
   305	}
   306	
   307	func (l *LabelsAllowList) String() string {
   308	        s := *l
   309	        ss := s.asSlice()
   310	        sort.Strings(ss)
   311	        return strings.Join(ss, ",")
   312	}

   315	func (l *LabelsAllowList) Type() string {
   316	        return "string"
   317	}

   105	// AddFlags populated the Options struct from the command line arguments passed.
   106	func (o *Options) AddFlags(cmd *cobra.Command) {
   107	        o.cmd = cmd
   108	
   109	        completionCommand.SetHelpFunc(func(_ *cobra.Command, _ []string) {
   110	                if shellPath, ok := os.LookupEnv("SHELL"); ok {
   111	                        shell := shellPath[strings.LastIndex(shellPath, "/")+1:]
   112	                        fmt.Println(FetchLoadInstructions(shell))
   113	                } else {
   114	                        fmt.Println("SHELL environment variable not set, falling back to bash")
   115	                        fmt.Println(FetchLoadInstructions("bash"))
   116	                }
   117	                klog.FlushAndExit(klog.ExitFlushTimeout, 0)
   118	        })
   119	
   120	        versionCommand := &cobra.Command{
   121	                Use:   "version",
   122	                Short: "Print version information.",
   123	                Run: func(_ *cobra.Command, _ []string) {
   124	                        fmt.Printf("%s\n", version.Print("kube-state-metrics"))
   125	                        klog.FlushAndExit(klog.ExitFlushTimeout, 0)
   126	                },
   127	        }
   128	
   129	        cmd.AddCommand(completionCommand, versionCommand)
   130	
   131	        o.cmd.Flags().Usage = func() {
   132	                _, _ = fmt.Fprintf(os.Stderr, "Usage of %s:\n", os.Args[0])
   133	                o.cmd.Flags().PrintDefaults()
   134	        }
   135	
   136	        klogFlags := flag.NewFlagSet("klog", flag.ExitOnError)
   137	        klog.InitFlags(klogFlags)
   138	        o.cmd.Flags().AddGoFlagSet(klogFlags)
   139	        _ = o.cmd.Flags().Lookup("logtostderr").Value.Set("true")
   140	        o.cmd.Flags().Lookup("logtostderr").DefValue = "true"
   141	        o.cmd.Flags().Lookup("logtostderr").NoOptDefVal = "true"

   143	        // Opt into the new klog behavior where -stderrthreshold is honored even
   144	        // when -logtostderr=true (see kubernetes/klog#212, kubernetes/klog#432).
   145	        _ = klogFlags.Set("legacy_stderr_threshold_behavior", "false") //nolint:errcheck

   147	
   148	        autoshardingNotice := "When set, it is expected that --pod and --pod-namespace are both set. Most likely this should be passed via the downward API. This is used for auto-detecting sharding. If set, this has preference over statically configured sharding. This is experimental, it may be removed without notice."
   149

   183	        o.cmd.Flags().Var(&o.Resources, "resources", fmt.Sprintf("Comma-separated list of resources to be enabled. Defaults to %q", &DefaultResources))

   186	        o.cmd.Flags().DurationVar(&o.ServerWriteTimeout, "server-write-timeout", defaultServerWriteTimeout, "The maximum duration before timing out writes of the response. Align with the scrape interval or timeout of scraping clients..")

   188	        o.cmd.Flags().DurationVar(&o.ServerReadHeaderTimeout, "server-read-header-timeout", defaultServerReadHeaderTimeout, "The maximum duration for reading the header of requests.")
   189	}
   190	
   191	// Parse parses the flag definitions from the argument list.
   192	func (o *Options) Parse() error {
   193	        err := o.cmd.Execute()
   194	        return err
   195	}
   196	
   197	// Usage is the function called when an error occurs while parsing flags.
   198	func (o *Options) Usage() {
   199	        _ = o.cmd.Flags().FlagUsages()
   200	}
   201	
   202	// Validate validates arguments
   203	func (o *Options) Validate() error {
   204	        shardableResource := "pods"
   205	        if o.Node == "" {
   206	                return nil
   207	        }
   208	        for _, x := range o.Resources.AsSlice() {
   209	                if x != shardableResource {
   210	                        return fmt.Errorf("resource %s can't be sharded by field selector spec.nodeName", x)
   211	                }
   212	        }
   213	
   214	        if o.AutoGoMemlimitRatio <= 0.0 || o.AutoGoMemlimitRatio > 1.0 {
   215	                return fmt.Errorf("value for --auto-gomemlimit-ratio=%f must be greater than 0 and less than or equal to 1", o.AutoGoMemlimitRatio)
   216	        }
   217	
   218	        if o.ObjectLimit < 0 {
   219	                return fmt.Errorf("value for --object-limit=%d must be equal or greater than 0", o.ObjectLimit)
   220	        }
   221	
   222	        return nil
   223	}
   224

   101	
   102	// FetchLoadInstructions returns instructions for enabling autocompletion for a particular shell.
   103	func FetchLoadInstructions(shell string) string {
   104	        switch shell {
   105	        case "zsh":
   106	                return autoloadZsh
   107	        case "bash":
   108	                return autoloadBash
   109	        case "fish":
   110	                return autoloadFish
   111	        default:
   112	                return ""
   113	        }
   114	}
   115	
   116	var completionCommand = &cobra.Command{
   117	        Use:                   "completion [bash|zsh|fish]",
   118	        Short:                 "Generate completion script for kube-state-metrics.",
   119	        DisableFlagsInUseLine: true,
   120	        Aliases:               []string{"comp", "c"},
   121	        ValidArgs:             []string{"bash", "zsh", "fish"},
   122	        Args:                  cobra.ExactArgs(1),
   123	        Run: func(cmd *cobra.Command, args []string) {
   124	                switch args[0] {
   125	                case "bash":
   126	                        _ = cmd.Root().GenBashCompletion(os.Stdout)
   127	                case "zsh":
   128	                        _ = cmd.Root().GenZshCompletion(os.Stdout)
   129	                case "fish":
   130	                        _ = cmd.Root().GenFishCompletion(os.Stdout, true)
   131	                }
   132	                klog.FlushAndExit(klog.ExitFlushTimeout, 0)
   133	        },
   134	        Example: "kube-state-metrics completion bash > /tmp/kube-state-metrics.bash && source /tmp/kube-state-metrics.bash # for shells compatible with bash",
   135	}

    27	func main() {
    28	        opts := options.NewOptions()
    29	        cmd := options.InitCommand
    30	        cmd.Run = func(_ *cobra.Command, _ []string) {
    31	                internal.RunKubeStateMetricsWrapper(opts)
    32	        }
    33	        opts.AddFlags(cmd)
    34	        if err := opts.Parse(); err != nil {
    35	                klog.FlushAndExit(klog.ExitFlushTimeout, 1)
    36	        }
    37	        if err := opts.Validate(); err != nil {
    38	                klog.ErrorS(err, "Validating options error")
    39	                klog.FlushAndExit(klog.ExitFlushTimeout, 1)
    40	        }

    23	        "path/filepath"
    24	        "time"
    25	
    26	        "github.com/fsnotify/fsnotify"
    27	        "github.com/spf13/viper"
    28	        "k8s.io/klog/v2"
    29	        yaml "sigs.k8s.io/yaml/goyaml.v3"
    30	
    31	        "k8s.io/kube-state-metrics/v2/pkg/app"
    32	        "k8s.io/kube-state-metrics/v2/pkg/options"
    33	)
    34	
    35	// RunKubeStateMetricsWrapper is a wrapper around KSM, delegated to the root command.
    36	func RunKubeStateMetricsWrapper(opts *options.Options) {
    37	
    38	        KSMRunOrDie := func(ctx context.Context) {
    39	                if err := app.RunKubeStateMetricsWrapper(ctx, opts); err != nil {
    40	                        klog.ErrorS(err, "Failed to run kube-state-metrics")
    41	                        klog.FlushAndExit(klog.ExitFlushTimeout, 1)
    42	                }
    43	        }
    44	
    45	        ctx, cancel := context.WithCancel(context.Background())
    46	        defer cancel()
    47	
    48	        if file := options.GetConfigFile(*opts); file != "" {
    49	                cfgViper := viper.New()
    50	                cfgViper.SetConfigType("yaml")
    51	                cfgViper.SetConfigFile(file)
    52	                var cfgViperReadInConfigErr error
    53	                if cfgViperReadInConfigErr = cfgViper.ReadInConfig(); cfgViperReadInConfigErr != nil {
    54	                        if errors.Is(cfgViperReadInConfigErr, viper.ConfigFileNotFoundError{}) {
    55	                                klog.ErrorS(cfgViperReadInConfigErr, "Options configuration file not found at startup", "file", file)
    56	                        } else if _, isNotExisterr := os.Stat(filepath.Clean(file)); isNotExisterr != nil {
    57	                                // TODO: Remove this check once viper.ConfigFileNotFoundError is working as expected, see this issue -
    58	                                // https://github.com/spf13/viper/issues/1783
    59	                                klog.ErrorS(isNotExisterr, "Options configuration file not found at startup", "file", file)
    60	                        } else {
    61	                                klog.ErrorS(cfgViperReadInConfigErr, "Error reading options configuration file", "file", file)
    62	                        }
    63	                        if !opts.ContinueWithoutConfig {
    64	                                klog.FlushAndExit(klog.ExitFlushTimeout, 1)
    65	                        }
    66	                }
    67	                cfgViper.OnConfigChange(func(e fsnotify.Event) {
    68	                        klog.InfoS("Changes detected", "name", e.Name)
    69	                        cancel()
    70	                        // Wait for the ports to be released.
    71	                        <-time.After(3 * time.Second)
    72	                        ctx, cancel = context.WithCancel(context.Background())
    73	                        go KSMRunOrDie(ctx)
    74	                })
    75	                cfgViper.WatchConfig()
    76	
    77	                if cfgViperReadInConfigErr == nil {
    78	                        // Merge configFile values with opts so we get the CustomResourceConfigFile from config as well
    79	                        configFile, err := os.ReadFile(filepath.Clean(file))
    80	                        if err != nil {
    81	                                klog.ErrorS(err, "failed to read options configuration file", "file", file)
    82	                        }
    83	
    84	                        yaml.Unmarshal(configFile, opts)
    85	                }
    86	        }
    87	        if opts.CustomResourceConfigFile != "" {
    88	                crcViper := viper.New()
    89	                crcViper.SetConfigType("yaml")
    90	                crcViper.SetConfigFile(opts.CustomResourceConfigFile)
    91	                if cfgViperReadInConfigErr := crcViper.ReadInConfig(); cfgViperReadInConfigErr != nil {
    92	                        if errors.Is(cfgViperReadInConfigErr, viper.ConfigFileNotFoundError{}) {
    93	                                klog.ErrorS(cfgViperReadInConfigErr, "Custom resource configuration file not found at startup", "file", opts.CustomResourceConfigFile)
    94	                        } else if _, isNotExisterr := os.Stat(filepath.Clean(opts.CustomResourceConfigFile)); isNotExisterr != nil {
    95	                                // Adding this check in addition to the above since viper.ConfigFileNotFoundError is not working as expected due to this issue -
    96	                                // https://github.com/spf13/viper/issues/1783
    97	                                klog.ErrorS(isNotExisterr, "Custom resource configuration file not found at startup", "file", opts.CustomResourceConfigFile)
    98	                        } else {
    99	                                klog.ErrorS(cfgViperReadInConfigErr, "Error reading Custom resource configuration file", "file", opts.CustomResourceConfigFile)
   100	                        }
   101	                        if !opts.ContinueWithoutCustomResourceConfigFile {
   102	                                klog.FlushAndExit(klog.ExitFlushTimeout, 1)
   103	                        }
   104	                }
   105	                crcViper.OnConfigChange(func(e fsnotify.Event) {
   106	                        klog.InfoS("Changes detected", "name", e.Name)
   107	                        cancel()
   108	                        // Wait for the ports to be released.
   109	                        <-time.After(3 * time.Second)
   110	                        ctx, cancel = context.WithCancel(context.Background())
   111	                        go KSMRunOrDie(ctx)
   112	                })
   113	                crcViper.WatchConfig()
   114	        }
   115	        if opts.Kubeconfig != "" {
   116	                kubecfgViper := viper.New()
   117	                kubecfgViper.SetConfigType("yaml")
   118	                kubecfgViper.SetConfigFile(opts.Kubeconfig)
   119	                if err := kubecfgViper.ReadInConfig(); err != nil {
   120	                        if errors.Is(err, viper.ConfigFileNotFoundError{}) {
   121	                                klog.ErrorS(err, "kubeconfig file not found", "file", opts.Kubeconfig)
   122	                        } else {
   123	                                klog.ErrorS(err, "Error reading kubeconfig file", "file", opts.Kubeconfig)
   124	                        }
   125	                        klog.FlushAndExit(klog.ExitFlushTimeout, 1)
   126	                }
   127	                kubecfgViper.OnConfigChange(func(e fsnotify.Event) {
   128	                        klog.InfoS("Changes detected", "name", e.Name)
   129	                        cancel()
   130	                        // Wait for the ports to be released.
   131	                        <-time.After(3 * time.Second)
   132	                        ctx, cancel = context.WithCancel(context.Background())
   133	                        go KSMRunOrDie(ctx)
   134	                })
   135	                kubecfgViper.WatchConfig()
   136	        }
   137	        klog.InfoS("Starting kube-state-metrics")
   138	        KSMRunOrDie(ctx)
   139	        select {}
   140	}
   141

Now I can see the issue! Let me look at the `Options` struct more carefully. In the `Options` struct (line 52-53 of `options.go`), there are two fields:

```go
CustomResourceConfig                    string   `yaml:"custom_resource_config"`
CustomResourceConfigFile                string   `yaml:"custom_resource_state_config_file"`
```

But in the CLI flags (line 164-165):
```go
o.cmd.Flags().StringVar(&o.CustomResourceConfig, "custom-resource-state-config", ...)
o.cmd.Flags().StringVar(&o.CustomResourceConfigFile, "custom-resource-state-config-file", ...)
```

Now look at what happens in `wrapper.go`:

1. At line 48-85, if a config file (`--config`) is specified, it reads it with viper and then unmarshals it into `opts` at line 84: `yaml.Unmarshal(configFile, opts)`

2. The yaml tags for these fields are:
   - `CustomResourceConfig`: `yaml:"custom_resource_config"`
   - `CustomResourceConfigFile`: `yaml:"custom_resource_state_config_file"`

Wait, but the PR description says the config option is called `custom_resource_config_file` (without "state"):

```yaml
custom_resource_config_file: "/etc/kube-state-metrics/custom-resource-config.yaml"
```

But the yaml tag says `custom_resource_state_config_file`. This mismatch is likely the issue! The config file uses `custom_resource_config_file` but the yaml tag expects `custom_resource_state_config_file`.

Let me check the PRs mentioned: #2705 and #2703. Let me look at what changed in the yaml tag.

Let me also check if there is a test file that shows the expected config format

    24	func TestOptionsParse(t *testing.T) {
    25	        tests := []struct {
    26	                Desc         string
    27	                Args         []string
    28	                ExpectsError bool
    29	        }{
    30	                {
    31	                        Desc:         "resources command line argument",
    32	                        Args:         []string{"./kube-state-metrics", "--resources=configmaps,pods"},
    33	                        ExpectsError: false,
    34	                },
    35	                {
    36	                        Desc:         "namespaces command line argument",
    37	                        Args:         []string{"./kube-state-metrics", "--namespaces=default,kube-system"},
    38	                        ExpectsError: false,
    39	                },
    40	                {
    41	                        Desc:         "foo command line argument",
    42	                        Args:         []string{"./kube-state-metrics", "--foo=bar,baz"},
    43	                        ExpectsError: true,
    44	                },
    45	        }
    46	
    47	        opts := NewOptions()
    48	        opts.AddFlags(InitCommand)
    49	
    50	        for _, test := range tests {
    51	                t.Run(test.Desc, func(t *testing.T) {
    52	                        os.Args = test.Args
    53	
    54	                        err := opts.Parse()
    55	
    56	                        if !test.ExpectsError && err != nil {
    57	                                t.Errorf("Error for test with description: %s: %v", test.Desc, err.Error())
    58	                        }
    59	
    60	                        if test.ExpectsError && err == nil {
    61	                                t.Errorf("Expected error for test with description: %s", test.Desc)
    62	                        }
    63	                })
    64	        }
    65	}

    24	func TestResourceSetSet(t *testing.T) {
    25	        tests := []struct {
    26	                Desc        string
    27	                Value       string
    28	                Wanted      ResourceSet
    29	                WantedError bool
    30	        }{
    31	                {
    32	                        Desc:        "empty resources",
    33	                        Value:       "",
    34	                        Wanted:      ResourceSet{},
    35	                        WantedError: false,
    36	                },
    37	                {
    38	                        Desc:  "normal resources",
    39	                        Value: "configmaps,cronjobs,daemonsets,deployments",
    40	                        Wanted: ResourceSet(map[string]struct{}{
    41	                                "configmaps":  {},
    42	                                "cronjobs":    {},
    43	                                "daemonsets":  {},
    44	                                "deployments": {},
    45	                        }),
    46	                        WantedError: false,
    47	                },
    48	        }
    49	
    50	        for _, test := range tests {
    51	                cs := &ResourceSet{}
    52	                gotError := cs.Set(test.Value)
    53	                if ((gotError != nil || test.WantedError) && (gotError == nil || !test.WantedError)) || !reflect.DeepEqual(*cs, test.Wanted) {
    54	                        t.Errorf("Test error for Desc: %s. Want: %+v. Got: %+v. Wanted Error: %v, Got Error: %v", test.Desc, test.Wanted, *cs, test.WantedError, gotError)
    55	                }
    56	        }
    57	}

    89	func TestNamespaceList_GetNamespaces(t *testing.T) {
    90	        tests := []struct {
    91	                Desc       string
    92	                Namespaces NamespaceList
    93	                Wanted     NamespaceList
    94	        }{
    95	                {
    96	                        Desc:       "empty DeniedNamespaces",

   116	                        t.Errorf("Test error for Desc: %s. Want: %+v. Got: %+v.", test.Desc, test.Wanted, allowedNamespaces)
   117	                }
   118	        }

   185	func TestMergeFieldSelectors(t *testing.T) {
   186	        tests := []struct {
   187	                Desc             string
   188	                Namespaces       NamespaceList
   189	                DeniedNamespaces NamespaceList
   190	                Node             NodeType
   191	                Wanted           string
   192	        }{
   193	                {
   194	                        Desc:             "empty DeniedNamespaces",
   195	                        Namespaces:       NamespaceList{"default", "kube-system"},
   196	                        DeniedNamespaces: NamespaceList{},
   197	                        Node:             "",
   198	                        Wanted:           "",
   199	                },
   200	                {
   201	                        Desc:             "all DeniedNamespaces",
   202	                        Namespaces:       DefaultNamespaces,
   203	                        DeniedNamespaces: NamespaceList{"some-system"},
   204	                        Node:             "",
   205	                        Wanted:           "metadata.namespace!=some-system",
   206	                },
   207	                {
   208	                        Desc:             "general case",
   209	                        Namespaces:       DefaultNamespaces,
   210	                        DeniedNamespaces: NamespaceList{"case1-system", "case2-system"},
   211	                        Node:             "",
   212	                        Wanted:           "metadata.namespace!=case1-system,metadata.namespace!=case2-system",
   213	                },
   214	                {
   215	                        Desc:             "empty DeniedNamespaces",
   216	                        Namespaces:       NamespaceList{"default", "kube-system"},
   217	                        DeniedNamespaces: NamespaceList{},
   218	                        Node:             "k8s-node-1",
   219	                        Wanted:           "spec.nodeName=k8s-node-1",
   220	                },
   221	                {
   222	                        Desc:             "all DeniedNamespaces",
   223	                        Namespaces:       DefaultNamespaces,
   224	                        DeniedNamespaces: NamespaceList{"some-system"},
   225	                        Node:             "k8s-node-1",
   226	                        Wanted:           "metadata.namespace!=some-system,spec.nodeName=k8s-node-1",
   227	                },
   228	                {
   229	                        Desc:             "general case",
   230	                        Namespaces:       DefaultNamespaces,
   231	                        DeniedNamespaces: NamespaceList{"case1-system", "case2-system"},
   232	                        Node:             "k8s-node-1",
   233	                        Wanted:           "metadata.namespace!=case1-system,metadata.namespace!=case2-system,spec.nodeName=k8s-node-1",
   234	                },
   235	        }
   236	
   237	        for _, test := range tests {
   238	                ns := test.Namespaces
   239	                deniedNS := test.DeniedNamespaces
   240	                selector1 := ns.GetExcludeNSFieldSelector(deniedNS)
   241	                selector2 := test.Node.GetNodeFieldSelector()
   242	                actual, err := MergeFieldSelectors([]string{selector1, selector2})
   243	                if err != nil {
   244	                        t.Errorf("Test error for Desc: %s. Can't merge field selector %v.", test.Desc, err)
   245	                }
   246	                if !reflect.DeepEqual(actual, test.Wanted) {
   247	                        t.Errorf("Test error for Desc: %s. Want: %+v. Got: %+v.", test.Desc, test.Wanted, actual)
   248	                }
   249	        }
   250	}

   252	func TestMetricSetSet(t *testing.T) {
   253	        tests := []struct {
   254	                Desc   string
   255	                Value  string
   256	                Wanted MetricSet
   257	        }{
   258	                {
   259	                        Desc:   "empty metrics",
   260	                        Value:  "",
   261	                        Wanted: MetricSet{},
   262	                },
   263	                {
   264	                        Desc:  "normal metrics",
   265	                        Value: "kube_cronjob_info, kube_cronjob_labels, kube_daemonset_labels",
   266	                        Wanted: MetricSet(map[string]struct{}{
   267	                                "kube_cronjob_info":     {},
   268	                                "kube_cronjob_labels":   {},
   269	                                "kube_daemonset_labels": {},
   270	                        }),
   271	                },
   272	                {
   273	                        Desc:  "newlines are ignored",
   274	                        Value: "\n^kube_.+_annotations$,\n   ^kube_secret_labels$\n",
   275	                        Wanted: MetricSet{
   276	                                "^kube_secret_labels$":  struct{}{},
   277	                                "^kube_.+_annotations$": struct{}{},
   278	                        },
   279	                },
   280	        }
   281	
   282	        for _, test := range tests {
   283	                ms := &MetricSet{}
   284	                gotError := ms.Set(test.Value)
   285	                if gotError != nil || !reflect.DeepEqual(*ms, test.Wanted) {
   286	                        t.Errorf("Test error for Desc: %s. Want: %+v. Got: %+v. Got Error: %v", test.Desc, test.Wanted, *ms, gotError)
   287	                }
   288	        }
   289	}
   290	
   291	func TestLabelsAllowListSet(t *testing.T) {
   292	        tests := []struct {
   293	                Desc   string
   294	                Value  string
   295	                Wanted LabelsAllowList
   296	                err    bool
   297	        }{
   298	                {
   299	                        Desc:   "empty labels list",
   300	                        Value:  "",
   301	                        Wanted: LabelsAllowList{},
   302	                },
   303	                {
   304	                        Desc:   "[invalid] space delimited",
   305	                        Value:  "cronjobs=[somelabel,label2] cronjobs=[label3,label4]",
   306	                        Wanted: LabelsAllowList(map[string][]string{}),
   307	                        err:    true,
   308	                },
   309	                {
   310	                        Desc:   "[invalid] normal missing bracket",
   311	                        Value:  "cronjobs=[somelabel,label2],cronjobs=label3,label4]",
   312	                        Wanted: LabelsAllowList(map[string][]string{}),
   313	                        err:    true,
   314	                },
   315	
   316	                {
   317	                        Desc:   "[invalid] no comma between metrics",
   318	                        Value:  "cronjobs=[somelabel,label2]cronjobs=[label3,label4]",
   319	                        Wanted: LabelsAllowList(map[string][]string{}),
   320	                        err:    true,
   321	                },
   322	                {
   323	                        Desc:   "[invalid] no '=' between name and label list",
   324	                        Value:  "cronjobs[somelabel,label2]cronjobs=[label3,label4]",
   325	                        Wanted: LabelsAllowList(map[string][]string{}),
   326	                        err:    true,
   327	                },
   328	                {
   329	                        Desc:  "one resource",
   330	                        Value: "cronjobs=[somelabel.io,label2/blah]",
   331	                        Wanted: LabelsAllowList(map[string][]string{
   332	                                "cronjobs": {
   333	                                        "somelabel.io",
   334	                                        "label2/blah",
   335	                                }}),
   336	                },
   337	                {
   338	                        Desc:  "two resources",
   339	                        Value: "pods=[podsone,pods-two],nodes=[nodesone,nodestwo],namespaces=[nsone,nstwo]",
   340	                        Wanted: LabelsAllowList(map[string][]string{
   341	                                "pods": {
   342	                                        "podsone",
   343	                                        "pods-two"},
   344	                                "nodes": {
   345	                                        "nodesone",
   346	                                        "nodestwo"},
   347	                                "namespaces": {
   348	                                        "nsone",
   349	                                        "nstwo"}}),
   350	                },
   351	                {
   352	                        Desc:  "with empty allow labels",
   353	                        Value: "cronjobs=[somelabel,label2],pods=[]",
   354	                        Wanted: LabelsAllowList(map[string][]string{
   355	                                "cronjobs": {
   356	                                        "somelabel",
   357	                                        "label2",
   358	                                },
   359	                                "pods": {}}),
   360	                },
   361	                {
   362	                        Desc:  "with wildcard",
   363	                        Value: "cronjobs=[*],pods=[*,foo],namespaces=[bar,*]",
   364	                        Wanted: LabelsAllowList(map[string][]string{
   365	                                "cronjobs": {
   366	                                        "*",
   367	                                },
   368	                                "pods": {
   369	                                        "*",
   370	                                        "foo",
   371	                                },
   372	                                "namespaces": {
   373	                                        "bar",
   374	                                        "*"}}),
   375	                },
   376	                {
   377	                        Desc:  "with key as wildcard",
   378	                        Value: "*=[*]",
   379	                        Wanted: LabelsAllowList(map[string][]string{
   380	                                "*": {
   381	                                        "*",
   382	                                },
   383	                        }),
   384	                },
   385	        }
   386	
   387	        for _, test := range tests {
   388	                lal := &LabelsAllowList{}
   389	                gotError := lal.Set(test.Value)
   390	                if gotError != nil && !test.err || !reflect.DeepEqual(*lal, test.Wanted) {
   391	                        t.Errorf("Test error for Desc: %s\n Want: \n%+v\n Got: \n%#+v\n Got Error: %#v", test.Desc, test.Wanted, *lal, gotError)
   392	                }
   393	        }
   394	}
   395

## v2.17.0 / 2025-09-01

* This release builds with Go `v1.24.6`
* This release builds with `k8s.io/client-go`: `v0.33.4`
* This release is the last release that has endpoint metrics enabled by default. In the next release we will enable endpointslices metrics and disable endpoint metrics by default, since the endpoint resources are deprecated. You can still alter this behaviour in kube-state-metrics' config.

* [FEATURE] Add new metric for pod unscheduled time tracking by @yshngg in <https://github.com/kubernetes/kube-state-metrics/pull/2699>
* [BUGFIX] Fix index out of range by @taraspos in <https://github.com/kubernetes/kube-state-metrics/pull/2716>
* [BUGFIX] Config file overrides apply to some fields but not other by @rashmichandrashekar in <https://github.com/kubernetes/kube-state-metrics/pull/2705>
* [BUGFIX] Fix logic for plain text fallback format by @timonegk in <https://github.com/kubernetes/kube-state-metrics/pull/2730>
* [FEATURE] Include reason label to `kube_deployment_status_condition` by @Rishab87 in <https://github.com/kubernetes/kube-state-metrics/pull/2719>
* [FEATURE] Continue running kube-state-metrics when config file doesnt exist at startup by @rashmichandrashekar in <https://github.com/kubernetes/kube-state-metrics/pull/2703>
* [FEATURE] Introduce deletion timestamp metric for daemonset, statefulset, deployment, service and pdb by @IgorIgnatevBolt in <https://github.com/kubernetes/kube-state-metrics/pull/2678>
* [FEATURE] Add HorizontalPodAutoscaler created and deletionTimestamp info into metrics by @IgorIgnatevBolt in <https://github.com/kubernetes/kube-state-metrics/pull/2675>

Now let me look at the `wrapper.go` more carefully. The issue is clear:

In `wrapper.go` at line 84:
```go
yaml.Unmarshal(configFile, opts)
```

This unmarshals the config YAML into the `Options` struct. But the yaml tag for `CustomResourceConfigFile` is `custom_resource_state_config_file`, while users expect `custom_resource_config_file` (as shown in the PR description).

Let me verify by creating a simple test:







🎬 ACTION
cd /testbed && cat > /tmp/test_yaml.go << 'EOF'
package main

import (
    "fmt"
    yaml "sigs.k8s.io/yaml/goyaml.v3"
)

type Options struct {
    CustomResourceConfig     string `yaml:"custom_resource_config"`
    CustomResourceConfigFile string `yaml:"custom_resource_state_config_file"`
}

func main() {
    configYAML := `
custom_resource_config_file: /etc/kube-state-metrics/custom-resource-config.yaml
`
    opts := &Options{}
    err := yaml.Unmarshal([]byte(configYAML), opts)
    if err != nil {
        fmt.Printf("Error: %v\n", err)
    }
    fmt.Printf("CustomResourceConfigFile: '%s'\n", opts.CustomResourceConfigFile)
    
    configYAML2 := `
custom_resource_state_config_file: /etc/kube-state-metrics/custom-resource-config.yaml
`
    opts2 := &Options{}
    err = yaml.Unmarshal([]byte(configYAML2), opts2)
    if err != nil {
        fmt.Printf("Error: %v\n", err)
    }
    fmt.Printf("CustomResourceConfigFile: '%s'\n", opts2.CustomResourceConfigFile)
}
EOF

- `custom_resource_config` (not `custom_resource_state_config`)

- `custom_resource_state_config_file` → `custom_resource_config_file`

package main

import (
    "fmt"
    yaml "sigs.k8s.io/yaml/goyaml.v3"
)

type Options struct {
    CustomResourceConfig                    string `yaml:"custom_resource_config"`
    CustomResourceConfigFile                string `yaml:"custom_resource_config_file"`
    ContinueWithoutCustomResourceConfigFile bool   `yaml:"continue_without_custom_resource_config_file"`
}

func main() {
    // Test 1: The user's config from the PR description
    configYAML := `
custom_resource_config_file: /etc/kube-state-metrics/custom-resource-config.yaml
`
    opts := &Options{}
    err := yaml.Unmarshal([]byte(configYAML), opts)
    if err != nil {
        fmt.Printf("Error: %v\n", err)
    }
    fmt.Printf("Test 1 - CustomResourceConfigFile: '%s'\n", opts.CustomResourceConfigFile)
    if opts.CustomResourceConfigFile == "/etc/kube-state-metrics/custom-resource-config.yaml" {
        fmt.Println("Test 1 PASSED")
    } else {
        fmt.Println("Test 1 FAILED")
    }

    // Test 2: The continue without option
    configYAML2 := `
custom_resource_config_file: ./my-config.yaml
continue_without_custom_resource_config_file: true
`
    opts2 := &Options{}
    err = yaml.Unmarshal([]byte(configYAML2), opts2)
    if err != nil {
        fmt.Printf("Error: %v\n", err)
    }
    fmt.Printf("Test 2 - CustomResourceConfigFile: '%s'\n", opts2.CustomResourceConfigFile)
    fmt.Printf("Test 2 - ContinueWithoutCustomResourceConfigFile: %v\n", opts2.ContinueWithoutCustomResourceConfigFile)
    if opts2.CustomResourceConfigFile == "./my-config.yaml" && opts2.ContinueWithoutCustomResourceConfigFile == true {
        fmt.Println("Test 2 PASSED")
    } else {
        fmt.Println("Test 2 FAILED")
    }

    // Test 3: Inline config still works
    configYAML3 := `
custom_resource_config: "inline yaml here"
`
    opts3 := &Options{}
    err = yaml.Unmarshal([]byte(configYAML3), opts3)
    if err != nil {
        fmt.Printf("Error: %v\n", err)
    }
    fmt.Printf("Test 3 - CustomResourceConfig: '%s'\n", opts3.CustomResourceConfig)
    if opts3.CustomResourceConfig == "inline yaml here" {
        fmt.Println("Test 3 PASSED")
    } else {
        fmt.Println("Test 3 FAILED")
    }
}
EOF

Usage:
  kube-state-metrics [command]

Available Commands:
  completion  Generate completion script for kube-state-metrics.
  help        Help about any command
  version     Print version information.

Flags:
      --add_dir_header                                       If true, adds the file directory to the header of the log messages
      --alsologtostderr                                      log to standard error as well as files (no effect when -logtostderr=true)
      --alsologtostderrthreshold severity                    logs at or above this threshold go to stderr when -alsologtostderr=true (no effect when -logtostderr=true)
      --apiserver string                                     The URL of the apiserver to use as a master
      --auth-filter                                          If true, requires authentication and authorization through Kubernetes API to access metrics endpoints
      --auto-gomemlimit                                      Automatically set GOMEMLIMIT to match container or system memory limit. (experimental)
      --auto-gomemlimit-ratio float                          The ratio of reserved GOMEMLIMIT memory to the detected maximum container or system memory. (experimental) (default 0.9)
      --config string                                        Path to the kube-state-metrics options config YAML file. If this flag is set, the flags defined in the file override the command line flags.
      --continue-without-config                              If true, kube-state-metrics continues to run even if the config file specified by --config is not present. This is useful for scenarios where config file is not provided at startup but is provided later, for e.g., via configmap. Kube-state-metrics will not exit with an error if the config file is not found, instead watches and reloads when it is created.
      --continue-without-custom-resource-state-config-file   If true, Kube-state-metrics continues to run even if the config file specified by --custom-resource-state-config-file is not present. This is useful for scenarios where config file is not provided at startup but is provided later, for e.g., via configmap. Kube-state-metrics will not exit with an error if the custom-resource-state-config file is not found, instead watches and reloads when it is created.
      --custom-resource-state-config string                  Inline Custom Resource State Metrics config YAML (experimental)
      --custom-resource-state-config-file string             Path to a Custom Resource State Metrics config file (experimental)
      --custom-resource-state-only                           Only provide Custom Resource State metrics (experimental)
      --enable-gzip-encoding                                 Gzip responses when requested by clients via 'Accept-Encoding: gzip' header.
  -h, --help                                                 Print Help text
      --host string                                          Host to expose metrics on. (default "::")
      --kubeconfig string                                    Absolute path to the kubeconfig file
      --legacy_stderr_threshold_behavior                     If true, stderrthreshold is ignored when logtostderr=true (legacy behavior). If false, stderrthreshold is honored even when logtostderr=true (default true)

      --logtostderr                                          log to standard error instead of files (default true)
      --metric-allowlist string                              Comma-separated list of metrics to be exposed. This list comprises of exact metric names and/or *ECMAScript-based* regex patterns. The allowlist and denylist are mutually exclusive.
      --metric-annotations-allowlist string                  Comma-separated list of Kubernetes annotations keys that will be used in the resource' labels metric. By default the annotations metrics are not exposed. To include them, provide a list of resource names in their plural form and Kubernetes annotation keys you would like to allow for them (Example: '=namespaces=[kubernetes.io/team,...],pods=[kubernetes.io/team],...)'. A single '*' can be provided per resource instead to allow any annotations, but that has severe performance implications (Example: '=pods=[*]').
      --metric-denylist string                               Comma-separated list of metrics not to be enabled. This list comprises of exact metric names and/or *ECMAScript-based* regex patterns. The allowlist and denylist are mutually exclusive.
      --metric-labels-allowlist string                       Comma-separated list of additional Kubernetes label keys that will be used in the resource' labels metric. By default the labels metrics are not exposed. To include them, provide a list of resource names in their plural form and Kubernetes label keys you would like to allow for them (Example: '=namespaces=[k8s-label-1,k8s-label-n,...],pods=[app],...)'. A single '*' can be provided per resource instead to allow any labels, but that has severe performance implications (Example: '=pods=[*]'). Additionally, an asterisk (*) can be provided as a key, which will resolve to all resources, i.e., assuming '--resources=deployments,pods', '=*=[*]' will resolve to '=deployments=[*],pods=[*]'.
      --metric-opt-in-list string                            Comma-separated list of metrics which are opt-in and not enabled by default. This is in addition to the metric allow- and denylists
      --namespaces string                                    Comma-separated list of namespaces to be enabled. Defaults to ""
      --namespaces-denylist string                           Comma-separated list of namespaces not to be enabled. If namespaces and namespaces-denylist are both set, only namespaces that are excluded in namespaces-denylist will be used.
      --node string                                          Name of the node that contains the kube-state-metrics pod. Most likely it should be passed via the downward API. This is experimental, it may be removed without notice.

Now let me think about edge cases. The fix changes the yaml tags so that:
1. `custom_resource_config_file` maps to `CustomResourceConfigFile` (the file-based config)
2. `continue_without_custom_resource_config_file` maps to `ContinueWithoutCustomResourceConfigFile`

These match what users expect based on the PR description.

One thing I want to double-check: the PR description shows the user using `custom_resource_config_file` (without "state") in their config.yaml. In v2.16.0, this worked. In v2.17.0, it broke because the yaml tag was changed to `custom_resource_state_config_file`. My fix reverts it back to `custom_resource_config_file`.

But I should also consider: what if someone has already updated their config to use `custom_resource_state_config_file` (the new, broken key) with v2.17.0? Well, since it was broken (the config file option didn't work at all in v2.17.0), nobody would have successfully used it. So reverting is safe.

However, to be extra safe and provide backward compatibility for both, we could support both yaml keys. But that would require custom unmarshaling logic. For now, the minimal fix is to revert the yaml tags to what they were before v2.17.0.

Let me now submit the solution.</think>The issue is clear. The yaml tags for `CustomResourceConfigFile` and `ContinueWithoutCustomResourceConfigFile` in the `Options` struct were changed in v2.17.0 to include "state" (e.g., `custom_resource_state_config_file`) to match the CLI flag names. However, users' existing config files use the keys without "state" (e.g., `custom_resource_config_file`), which is what worked in v2.16.0.

The fix reverts the yaml tags back to their pre-2.17.0 values:

1. `CustomResourceConfigFile` yaml tag: `custom_resource_state_config_file` → `custom_resource_config_file`
2. `ContinueWithoutCustomResourceConfigFile` yaml tag: `continue_without_custom_resource_state_config_file` → `continue_without_custom_resource_config_file`

This ensures that the config file option `custom_resource_config_file` works as expected, matching the behavior from v2.16.0.

-		}
-	}

+        shardableResource := "pods"
+        if o.Node == "" {
+                return nil
+        }
+        for _, x := range o.Resources.AsSlice() {
+                if x != shardableResource {
+                        return fmt.Errorf("resource %s can't be sharded by field selector spec.nodeName", x)

+        }
+

+

+                return fmt.Errorf("value for --object-limit=%d must be equal or greater than 0", o.ObjectLimit)
+        }

+        return nil

 // Validate validates arguments
 func (o *Options) Validate() error {
-	shardableResource := "pods"
-	if o.Node == "" {
-		return nil
-	}
-	for _, x := range o.Resources.AsSlice() {
-		if x != shardableResource {
-			return fmt.Errorf("resource %s can't be sharded by field selector spec.nodeName", x)
-		}
-	}
-
-	if o.AutoGoMemlimitRatio <= 0.0 || o.AutoGoMemlimitRatio > 1.0 {
-		return fmt.Errorf("value for --auto-gomemlimit-ratio=%f must be greater than 0 and less than or equal to 1", o.AutoGoMemlimitRatio)
-	}
-

-		return fmt.Errorf("value for --object-limit=%d must be equal or greater than 0", o.ObjectLimit)

+        shardableResource := "pods"
+        if o.Node == "" {
+                return nil
+        }
+        for _, x := range o.Resources.AsSlice() {
+                if x != shardableResource {
+                        return fmt.Errorf("resource %s can't be sharded by field selector spec.nodeName", x)
+                }
+        }
+

+        }
+
+        if o.ObjectLimit < 0 {
+                return fmt.Errorf("value for --object-limit=%d must be equal or greater than 0", o.ObjectLimit)
+        }
+
+        return nil
 }
